RE 26381 V─Бtul─Бgama. There are 63 folios in this bundle. The conditions of folios are very good. Around 7/8 lines and 50 characters in each lines are there on each side of folios. Size of the manuscript 14 x 2. This bundle deals with few paс╣нalas of V─Бtul─Бgma which is one of the 28 Siddh─Бntha ┼Ыaiva m┼лl─Бgamas. The ┼Ыrot─Б means, the receivers of this ─Бgama is с╣гanmukha. As per the K─Бmik─Бgama the ┼Ыrot─Б should be ┼Ыiva and mah─Бk─Бla but here are some changes. There are 12 up─Бgamas for this m┼лl─Бgama, namely v─Бtulam, v─Бtulottaram, k─Бlaj├▒─Бnam, prarohitam, sarvam, dharm─Бtmakam, с╣Зityam, ┼Ыreс╣гс╣нam, ┼Ыuddham, mah─Бnanam, vi┼Ыvam and Vvi┼Ыv─Бtmakam. This bundle mainly contains the Nity─Бrcan─Бvidhipaс╣нala, the p┼лj─Бwhich is done by the priest in all the days for the sake of lOkakaly─Бnam Multiverse. The other related topics in the paс╣нala are ┼Ыivaliс╣Еg─Бrcanam, ┼Ыauc─Бdi-nityakarma, nitya-naimittika-k─Бmya-p┼лj─Б, utsavaviс╣гayaс╕е, pr─Бya┼Ыcittaviс╣гayaс╕е and there difference in musical instruments and flowers etc.
